FROM [Tasks] AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[CreatedAt], [p].[DeletedAt], [p].[Description], [p].[EndDate], [p].[IsDeleted], [p].[Name], [p].[StartDate], [p].[Status], [p].[UpdatedAt]
    FROM [Projects] AS [p]
    WHERE [p].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [t0] ON [t].[ProjectId] = [t0].[Id]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [e].[Id], [e].[BasicSalary], [e].[CreatedAt], [e].[DeletedAt], [e].[DepartmentId], [e].[DesignationId], [e].[Email], [e].[FullName], [e].[HireDate], [e].[IsActive], [e].[IsDeleted], [e].[PhoneNumber], [e].[PhotoPath], [e].[TrainingProgramId], [e].[UpdatedAt], [e].[UserId]
